Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/containerd--317286ac`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--8c9c67c0`

Trace the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition to containerd's implementation

The Kubernetes CRI defines a gRPC RuntimeService in its api.proto file. Trace the complete interface contract:
1. Find the CRI RuntimeService gRPC definition in the kubernetes repo (under staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/)
2. Identify the key RPC methods (RunPodSandbox, StopPodSandbox, RemovePodSandbox, etc.)
3. Find where containerd implements these CRI methods
4. Document how kubernetes vendors containerd's API types (check kubernetes/vendor/github.com/containerd/)

Your analysis must span both the kubernetes and containerd source trees under /ccb_crossrepo/src/.
Write your findings to REASONING.md in the workspace.

62-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've created a comprehensive analysis document that traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition through containerd's implementation.

## Summary of the Analysis

The **REASONING.md** file documents:

### 1. **CRI RuntimeService Definition** (Kubernetes)
- Located in `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`
- Defines 30+ RPC methods for pod sandbox and container lifecycle management
- Key operations: RunPodSandbox, StopPodSandbox, RemovePodSandbox, CreateContainer, StartContainer, etc.

### 2. **Key RPC Methods Identified**
- **RunPodSandbox**: Creates and starts a pod-level sandbox
- **StopPodSandbox**: Stops running processes and reclaims network resources (idempotent)
- **RemovePodSandbox**: Removes sandbox and all containers (idempotent)
- **PodSandboxStatus**: Returns sandbox state
- **Container operations**: Create, start, stop, remove, exec, attach, stats

### 3. **Containerd Implementation**
- **Plugin layer** (`plugins/cri/cri.go`): Registers as a gRPC plugin, embeds RuntimeServiceServer and ImageServiceServer
- **Service layer** (`internal/cri/server/service.go`): criService struct with state management
- **Implementation files**:
  - `sandbox_run.go`: RunPodSandbox - creates leases, reserves names, starts sandboxes
  - `sandbox_stop.go`: StopPodSandbox - stops containers then sandbox (idempotent)
  - `sandbox_remove.go`: RemovePodSandbox - cleans up all resources

### 4. **Interface Contract Semantics**
- **Idempotent operations**: StopPodSandbox and RemovePodSandbox return success even if resource not found
- **Cascading lifecycle**: Containers stopped before sandbox, containers removed before sandbox
- **Error handling**: Distinguishes between "not found" (success) and real errors
- **Re
... (truncated)

mode.\n924:     // Privileged mode is incompatible with the following options. If\n925:     // privileged is set, the following features MAY have no effect:\n926:     // 1. capabilities\n927:     // 2. selinux_options\n928:     // 4. seccomp\n929:     // 5. apparmor\n930:     //\n931:     // Privileged mode implies the following specific options are applied:\n932:     // 1. {
  "content": "# Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) Trace Analysis\n\n## Overview\n\nThis document traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition through containerd's implementation. The analysis spans both the Kubernetes and containerd repositories, mapping the interface contract to concrete implementation.\n\n---\n\n## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition\n\n### 1.1 Definition Location\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n\nThe Kubernetes project maintains the Container Runtime Interface as a protocol buffer specification with gRPC service definitions. This is the source of truth for all container runtime implementations.\n\n### 1.2 Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService\n\nThe CRI RuntimeService gRPC interface defines the following key RPC methods:\n\n#### Sandbox Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\nservice RuntimeService {\n    // Version returns the runtime name, runtime version, and runtime API version.\n    rpc Version(VersionRequest) returns (VersionResponse) {}\n\n    // RunPodSandbox creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes must ensure\n    // the sandbox is in the ready state on success.\n    rpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // StopPodSandbox stops any running process that is part of the sandbox and\n    // reclaims network resources (e.g., IP addresses) allocated to the sandbox.\n    // If there are any running containers in the sandbox, they must be forcibly\n    // terminated. This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if all\n    // relevant resources have already been reclaimed.\n    rpc StopPodSandbox(StopPodSandboxRequest) returns (StopPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // RemovePodSandbox removes the sandbox. If there are any running containers\n    // in the sandbox, they must be forcibly terminated and removed.\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the sandbox has\n    // already been removed.\n    rpc RemovePodSandbox(RemovePodSandboxRequest) returns (RemovePodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStatus returns the status of the PodSandbox. If the PodSandbox is\n    // not present, returns an error.\n    rpc PodSandboxStatus(PodSandboxStatusRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandbox returns a list of PodSandboxes.\n    rpc ListPodSandbox(ListPodSandboxRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n#### Container Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\n    // CreateContainer creates a new container in specified PodSandbox\n    rpc CreateContainer(CreateContainerRequest) returns (CreateContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StartContainer starts the container.\n    rpc StartContainer(StartContainerRequest) returns (StartContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StopContainer stops a running container with a grace period (i.e., timeout).\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the container has\n    // already been stopped.\n    rpc StopContainer(StopContainerRequest) returns (StopContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveContainer removes the container. If the container is running, the\n    // container must be forcibly removed.\n    rpc RemoveContainer(RemoveContainerRequest) returns (RemoveContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainers lists all containers by filters.\n    rpc ListContainers(ListContainersRequest) returns (ListContainersResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStatus returns status of the container. If the container is not\n    // present, returns an error.\n    rpc ContainerStatus(ContainerStatusRequest) returns (ContainerStatusResponse) {}\n```\n\n#### Advanced Operations\n```protobuf\n    // ExecSync runs a command in a container synchronously.\n    rpc ExecSync(ExecSyncRequest) returns (ExecSyncResponse) {}\n\n    // Exec prepares a streaming endpoint to execute a command in the container.\n    rpc Exec(ExecRequest) returns (ExecResponse) {}\n\n    // Attach prepares a streaming endpoint to attach to a running container.\n    rpc Attach(AttachRequest) returns (AttachResponse) {}\n\n    // PortForward prepares a streaming endpoint to forward ports from a PodSandbox.\n    rpc PortForward(PortForwardRequest) returns (PortForwardResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStats returns stats of the container.\n    rpc ContainerStats(ContainerStatsRequest) returns (ContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainerStats returns stats of all running containers.\n    rpc ListContainerStats(ListContainerStatsRequest) returns (ListContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandbox.\n    rpc PodSandboxStats(PodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandboxes matching a filter.\n    rpc ListPodSandboxStats(ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // Status returns the status of the runtime.\n    rpc Status(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse) {}\n\n    // GetContainerEvents gets container events from the CRI runtime\n    rpc GetContainerEvents(GetEventsRequest) returns (stream ContainerEventResponse) {}\n```\n\n### 1.3 ImageService gRPC Definition\n\nThe CRI also defines an ImageService interface:\n\n```protobuf\nservice ImageService {\n    // ListImages lists existing images.\n    rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageStatus returns the status of the image. If the image is not present,\n    // returns a response with ImageStatusResponse.Image set to nil.\n    rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // PullImage pulls an image with authentication config.\n    rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveImage removes the image.\n    rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageFSInfo returns information of the filesystem that is used to store images.\n    rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Message Type Hierarchy\n\nThe proto definitions include structured message types that form a clear contract:\n\n### Pod Sandbox Messages\n- `RunPodSandboxRequest` / `RunPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Contains `PodSandboxConfig` with metadata, network config, DNS, Linux config, etc.\n  - Returns the sandbox ID as a string\n- `StopPodSandboxRequest` / `StopPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `RemovePodSandboxRequest` / `RemovePodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `PodSandboxStatus` message contains:\n  - Sandbox ID, state, creation timestamp\n  - Network settings, metadata labels\n  - Linux-specific namespace paths\n\n### Container Messages\n- `CreateContainerRequest` / `CreateContainerResponse`\n- `StartContainerRequest` / `StartContainerResponse`\n- `ContainerStatus` contains state (created, running, exited) and detailed resource info\n\n---\n\n## 3. Generated gRPC Code\n\n### 3.1 gRPC Compilation\nThe proto files are compiled to generate:\n- **File**: `api_grpc.pb.go` - Contains the gRPC service definitions\n- Generated client interface: `RuntimeServiceClient`\n- Generated server interface: `RuntimeServiceServer`\n- Method handlers and registration functions\n\n### 3.2 Server Interface Example\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    Version(context.Context, *VersionRequest) (*VersionResponse, error)\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    StopPodSandbox(context.Context, *StopPodSandboxRequest) (*StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    RemovePodSandbox(context.Context, *RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*RemovePodSandboxResponse, error)\n    PodSandboxStatus(context.Context, *PodSandboxStatusRequest) (*PodSandboxStatusResponse, error)\n    // ... other methods\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Registration Function\n```go\nfunc RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s grpc.ServiceRegistrar, srv RuntimeServiceServer) {\n    // Registers all RPC handlers with the gRPC server\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### 4.1 Entry Point: CRI Plugin Registration\n\n**File**: `plugins/cri/cri.go` (containerd repository)\n\nThe containerd CRI plugin is initialized as a gRPC plugin:\n\n```go\nfunc init() {\n    defaultConfig := criconfig.DefaultServerConfig()\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,      // Runtime service\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,      // Sandbox controller\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,          // Node Resource Interface\n            plugins.EventPlugin,\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,\n        },\n        InitFn: initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 gRPC Server Implementation\n\n**Type**: `criGRPCServer` struct\n\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Embedded interface implementation\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer    // Embedded interface implementation\n    io.Closer\n    initializer                   // IsInitialized() method\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\nThis structure:\n- **Embeds** the gRPC server interfaces from the CRI API\n- **Wraps** them with instrumentation for logging, metrics, and tracing\n- **Registers** both services with the gRPC server\n\n### 4.3 Service Implementation Layer\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe actual implementation is in the `criService` struct:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    RuntimeService    // Embedded dependency\n    ImageService      // Embedded dependency\n\n    // State management\n    config             criconfig.Config\n    sandboxStore       *sandboxstore.Store    // Stores pod sandbox metadata\n    containerStore     *containerstore.Store  // Stores container metadata\n    sandboxNameIndex   *registrar.Registrar   // Ensures unique names\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n\n    // Network and streaming\n    netPlugin          map[string]cni.CNI    // CNI plugin for networking\n    streamServer       streaming.Server      // For exec/attach streams\n\n    // Monitoring and integration\n    eventMonitor       *events.EventMonitor  // Container event tracking\n    nri                *nri.API              // Node Resource Interface\n    sandboxService     sandboxService        // Sandbox controller\n    runtimeHandlers    map[string]*runtime.RuntimeHandler\n    statsCollector     *StatsCollector\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 Method Implementation Example: RunPodSandbox\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n\n    // 1. Generate unique ID and reserve name to prevent concurrent creation\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    metadata := config.GetMetadata()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n\n    if err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name: %w\", err)\n    }\n    defer func() {\n        if retErr != nil {\n            c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(name)\n        }\n    }()\n\n    // 2. Create lease for resource tracking\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    ls, err := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create lease: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Select OCI runtime based on config and runtime handler\n    ociRuntime, err := c.config.GetSandboxRuntime(config, r.GetRuntimeHandler())\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to get OCI runtime: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 4. Create sandbox store entry\n    sandbox := sandboxstore.NewSandbox(\n        sandboxstore.Metadata{\n            ID:             id,\n            Name:           name,\n            Config:         config,\n            RuntimeHandler: r.GetRuntimeHandler(),\n        },\n        sandboxstore.Status{\n            State: sandboxstore.StateUnknown,\n        },\n    )\n\n    // 5. Set up networking (CNI)\n    // 6. Start the sandbox via sandbox controller\n    // 7. Trigger NRI hooks for Node Resource Interface\n\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{\n        PodSandboxId: id,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Patterns:\n- **Resource isolation**: Each sandbox gets a lease for resource cleanup\n- **Name reservation**: Prevents concurrent creation of same sandbox\n- **Store management**: Maintains metadata in `sandboxStore` for lifecycle tracking\n- **Error recovery**: Deferred cleanup functions ensure partial failures are rolled back\n- **Instrumentation**: Wrapped with tracing spans and logging\n\n### 4.5 StopPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Look up sandbox in store (idempotent - returns success if not found)\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            // Idempotent: already stopped/removed, return success\n            return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error finding sandbox: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 2. Stop all containers in the sandbox (forced termination)\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.stopContainerRetryOnConnectionClosed(ctx, container, 0); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Stop the sandbox container itself if running or unknown\n    state := sandbox.Status.Get().State\n    if state == sandboxstore.StateReady || state == sandboxstore.StateUnknown {\n        if err := c.sandboxService.StopSandbox(ctx, sandbox.Sandboxer, sandbox.ID); err != nil {\n            if !errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop sandbox: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 4. Trigger NRI hooks\n    // 5. Update sandbox state to \"NotReady\"\n\n    return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Points:\n- **Idempotent semantics**: Returns success even if sandbox already stopped\n- **Cascading shutdown**: Stops all containers first, then the sandbox\n- **State tracking**: Uses internal state to avoid redundant operations\n- **Error handling**: Distinguishes between \"not found\" (ok) and real errors\n\n### 4.6 RemovePodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Find the sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // 2. Force-remove all containers in the sandbox\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.removeContainer(ctx, container.ID); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to remove container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Trigger NRI removal hooks\n    // 4. Release the sandbox name from the index\n    // 5. Delete lease\n    // 6. Remove from sandbox store\n\n    return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Instrumentation Layer\n\n### 5.1 Middleware Pattern\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go`\n\nContainerd wraps the criService with an instrumented service that adds:\n\n```go\ntype instrumentedService struct {\n    c runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Wrapped service\n}\n\nfunc (in *instrumentedService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Check if service is initialized\n    if err := in.checkInitialized(); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // Log the request\n    log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox for %+v\", r.GetConfig().GetMetadata())\n\n    // Call the actual implementation\n    res, err := in.c.RunPodSandbox(ctx, r)\n\n    // Log the response or error\n    if err != nil {\n        log.G(ctx).WithError(err).Errorf(\"RunPodSandbox failed\")\n    } else {\n        log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox returns sandbox id %q\", res.GetPodSandboxId())\n    }\n\n    return res, err\n}\n```\n\nThis pattern provides:\n- **Logging**: Detailed request/response logging\n- **Metrics**: Request timing and counts\n- **Tracing**: Distributed tracing spans\n- **Validation**: Server initialization checks\n\n---\n\n## 6. Kubernetes Vendoring of Containerd APIs\n\n### 6.1 Vendor Structure\n\n**Location**: `vendor/github.com/containerd/` (in kubernetes repo)\n\nKubernetes vendors only the **API types** from containerd, not the full implementation:\n\n```\nvendor/github.com/containerd/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 containerd/\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 api/\n\u2502       \u251c\u2500\u2500 services/      # gRPC service definitions\n\u2502       \u2514\u2500\u2500 types/         # Common data types\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 errdefs/              # Error definitions\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 log/                  # Logging interface\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 ttrpc/               # ttrpc protocol implementation\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 typeurl/             # Type URL registry for protobuf\n```\n\n### 6.2 Key Vendored Components\n\n**containerd/api/types**: Core container and sandbox types that represent the container runtime state\n\n**containerd/errdefs**: Error codes that containerd uses:\n- `IsNotFound(err)` - checks if resource doesn't exist\n- `IsAlreadyExists(err)` - resource creation collision\n- `IsInvalidArgument(err)` - malformed request\n- `IsFailedPrecondition(err)` - resource in wrong state\n\nThis error package is critical for the idempotent semantics of CRI operations.\n\n### 6.3 Kubernetes CRI Client\n\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`\n\nKubernetes implements a client that communicates with containerd via the CRI interface:\n\n```go\ntype remoteRuntimeService struct {\n    runtimeClient runtimeapi.RuntimeServiceClient  // gRPC client\n    timeout       time.Duration\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        config *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig, runtimeHandler string) (string, error) {\n\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    resp, err := r.runtimeClient.RunPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.RunPodSandboxRequest{\n        Config:         config,\n        RuntimeHandler: runtimeHandler,\n    })\n\n    if err != nil {\n        return \"\", err\n    }\n\n    return resp.PodSandboxId, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, podSandBoxID string) error {\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    _, err := r.runtimeClient.StopPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.StopPodSandboxRequest{\n        PodSandboxId: podSandBoxID,\n    })\n\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Interface Contract and Semantics\n\n### 7.1 Idempotent Operations\n\nBoth `StopPodSandbox` and `RemovePodSandbox` are **idempotent**:\n- Multiple calls with same ID should succeed\n- Calling on non-existent resource should return success\n- Kubelet relies on this for reliable cleanup\n\n**Implementation guarantee**: In both containerd and Kubernetes client:\n```\nif err != nil && !isNotFound(err) {\n    return err\n}\n// Return success regardless\n```\n\n### 7.2 Cascading Lifecycle\n\nThe CRI defines a specific lifecycle:\n1. **RunPodSandbox** - Creates and starts sandbox (must be Ready)\n2. **CreateContainer** - Creates containers in the sandbox\n3. **StartContainer** - Starts the containers\n4. **StopContainer** - Stops containers gracefully\n5. **StopPodSandbox** - Stops sandbox (must terminate all containers)\n6. **RemoveContainer** - Removes container metadata\n7. **RemovePodSandbox** - Removes sandbox metadata\n\nContainerd enforces this through state tracking and cascading cleanup.\n\n### 7.3 Graceful vs Forced Termination\n\n- **StopContainer(grace_period)**: Sends SIGTERM, waits for grace period, then SIGKILL\n- **StopPodSandbox**: Forcibly terminates all containers (grace period = 0)\n- **RemovePodSandbox**: Forcibly removes all containers\n\n### 7.4 Resource Cleanup\n\nThree levels of resource management:\n1. **Leases** (containerd): Automatic cleanup of orphaned resources\n2. **Stores** (criService): In-memory tracking of sandbox/container metadata\n3. **CNI plugins**: Network namespace cleanup on sandbox removal\n\n---\n\n## 8. Message Flow Example: Create and Run Pod\n\n### Complete Request-Response Chain\n\n```\nKubelet Requests:\n1. RunPodSandbox(config)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.RunPodSandbox()\n   \u2192 Creates lease, reserves name, creates sandbox store entry\n   \u2192 Calls sandboxService.StartSandbox() with OCI runtime\n   \u2192 Returns sandbox_id\n   Response: RunPodSandboxResponse { pod_sandbox_id = \"abc123\" }\n\n2. CreateContainer(sandbox_id, config)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.CreateContainer()\n   \u2192 Creates container store entry\n   \u2192 Generates OCI spec from config\n   Response: CreateContainerResponse { container_id = \"def456\" }\n\n3. StartContainer(container_id)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.StartContainer()\n   \u2192 Calls sandboxService.StartTask() to run OCI runtime\n   Response: StartContainerResponse {}\n\n4. PodSandboxStatus(sandbox_id)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.PodSandboxStatus()\n   \u2192 Returns sandbox state from store\n   Response: PodSandboxStatusResponse { status = SANDBOX_READY, ... }\n\nLater for cleanup:\n5. StopContainer(container_id, grace_period)\n   \u2192 Sends SIGTERM, waits, then SIGKILL\n   Response: StopContainerResponse {}\n\n6. RemoveContainer(container_id)\n   Response: RemoveContainerResponse {}\n\n7. StopPodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   \u2192 Stops all containers in sandbox\n   \u2192 Stops sandbox container\n   Response: StopPodSandboxResponse {}\n\n8. RemovePodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   \u2192 Removes all containers\n   \u2192 Releases name reservation\n   \u2192 Deletes lease\n   \u2192 Removes from store\n   Response: RemovePodSandboxResponse {}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Error Handling\n\n### 9.1 Error Types from Kubernetes CRI Spec\n\nAll operations return gRPC errors that map to error codes:\n- `Unimplemented` - Method not supported\n- `Internal` - Unexpected runtime error\n- `InvalidArgument` - Bad request parameters\n- `AlreadyExists` - Resource already created\n- `NotFound` - Resource doesn't exist\n- `FailedPrecondition` - Resource in wrong state\n\n### 9.2 Idempotency Handling\n\nContainerd's idempotent error handling:\n```go\n// In StopPodSandbox\nsandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(id)\nif err != nil {\n    if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n        return &StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil  // Success even if not found\n    }\n    return nil, err  // Real error\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Architecture Summary\n\n### 10.1 Layered Design\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Kubernetes kubelet                              \u2502\n\u2502 (CRI client - runtime.RuntimeServiceClient)     \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                   \u2502 gRPC calls over Unix socket\n                   \u2502\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25bc\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Containerd CRI Plugin (plugins/cri/cri.go)      \u2502\n\u2502 \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510   \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502 criGRPCServer                            \u2502   \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502 - Containerd's implementation demonstrates:\n\n1. **Correct semantics**: Implements idempotent operations as specified\n2. **Robust state management**: Uses stores and leases to prevent resource leaks\n3. **Graceful error handling**: Distinguishes between expected and unexpected errors\n4. **Extensibility**: Supports runtime selection, plugins (NRI), and event streaming\n5. **Observability**: Multi-layer instrumentation for debugging and monitoring\n\nThe interface contract is enforced through gRPC's strongly-typed message definitions, allowing Kubernetes and containerd to evolve independently while maintaining compatibility through the CRI protocol versioning system.\n",

  "content": "# Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) Trace Analysis\n\n## Overview\n\nThis document traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition through containerd's implementation. The analysis spans both the Kubernetes and containerd repositories, mapping the interface contract to concrete implementation.\n\n---\n\n## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition\n\n### 1.1 Definition Location\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n\nThe Kubernetes project maintains the Container Runtime Interface as a protocol buffer specification with gRPC service definitions. This is the source of truth for all container runtime implementations.\n\n### 1.2 Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService\n\nThe CRI RuntimeService gRPC interface defines the following key RPC methods:\n\n#### Sandbox Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\nservice RuntimeService {\n    // Version returns the runtime name, runtime version, and runtime API version.\n    rpc Version(VersionRequest) returns (VersionResponse) {}\n\n    // RunPodSandbox creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes must ensure\n    // the sandbox is in the ready state on success.\n    rpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // StopPodSandbox stops any running process that is part of the sandbox and\n    // reclaims network resources (e.g., IP addresses) allocated to the sandbox.\n    // If there are any running containers in the sandbox, they must be forcibly\n    // terminated. This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if all\n    // relevant resources have already been reclaimed.\n    rpc StopPodSandbox(StopPodSandboxRequest) returns (StopPodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // RemovePodSandbox removes the sandbox. If there are any running containers\n    // in the sandbox, they must be forcibly terminated and removed.\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the sandbox has\n    // already been removed.\n    rpc RemovePodSandbox(RemovePodSandboxRequest) returns (RemovePodSandboxResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStatus returns the status of the PodSandbox. If the PodSandbox is\n    // not present, returns an error.\n    rpc PodSandboxStatus(PodSandboxStatusRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandbox returns a list of PodSandboxes.\n    rpc ListPodSandbox(ListPodSandboxRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n#### Container Lifecycle Operations\n```protobuf\n    // CreateContainer creates a new container in specified PodSandbox\n    rpc CreateContainer(CreateContainerRequest) returns (CreateContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StartContainer starts the container.\n    rpc StartContainer(StartContainerRequest) returns (StartContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // StopContainer stops a running container with a grace period (i.e., timeout).\n    // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the container has\n    // already been stopped.\n    rpc StopContainer(StopContainerRequest) returns (StopContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveContainer removes the container. If the container is running, the\n    // container must be forcibly removed.\n    rpc RemoveContainer(RemoveContainerRequest) returns (RemoveContainerResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainers lists all containers by filters.\n    rpc ListContainers(ListContainersRequest) returns (ListContainersResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStatus returns status of the container. If the container is not\n    // present, returns an error.\n    rpc ContainerStatus(ContainerStatusRequest) returns (ContainerStatusResponse) {}\n```\n\n#### Advanced Operations\n```protobuf\n    // ExecSync runs a command in a container synchronously.\n    rpc ExecSync(ExecSyncRequest) returns (ExecSyncResponse) {}\n\n    // Exec prepares a streaming endpoint to execute a command in the container.\n    rpc Exec(ExecRequest) returns (ExecResponse) {}\n\n    // Attach prepares a streaming endpoint to attach to a running container.\n    rpc Attach(AttachRequest) returns (AttachResponse) {}\n\n    // PortForward prepares a streaming endpoint to forward ports from a PodSandbox.\n    rpc PortForward(PortForwardRequest) returns (PortForwardResponse) {}\n\n    // ContainerStats returns stats of the container.\n    rpc ContainerStats(ContainerStatsRequest) returns (ContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListContainerStats returns stats of all running containers.\n    rpc ListContainerStats(ListContainerStatsRequest) returns (ListContainerStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // PodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandbox.\n    rpc PodSandboxStats(PodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // ListPodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandboxes matching a filter.\n    rpc ListPodSandboxStats(ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n\n    // Status returns the status of the runtime.\n    rpc Status(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse) {}\n\n    // GetContainerEvents gets container events from the CRI runtime\n    rpc GetContainerEvents(GetEventsRequest) returns (stream ContainerEventResponse) {}\n```\n\n### 1.3 ImageService gRPC Definition\n\nThe CRI also defines an ImageService interface:\n\n```protobuf\nservice ImageService {\n    // ListImages lists existing images.\n    rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageStatus returns the status of the image. If the image is not present,\n    // returns a response with ImageStatusResponse.Image set to nil.\n    rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse) {}\n\n    // PullImage pulls an image with authentication config.\n    rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse) {}\n\n    // RemoveImage removes the image.\n    rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse) {}\n\n    // ImageFSInfo returns information of the filesystem that is used to store images.\n    rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse) {}\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Message Type Hierarchy\n\nThe proto definitions include structured message types that form a clear contract:\n\n### Pod Sandbox Messages\n- `RunPodSandboxRequest` / `RunPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Contains `PodSandboxConfig` with metadata, network config, DNS, Linux config, etc.\n  - Returns the sandbox ID as a string\n- `StopPodSandboxRequest` / `StopPodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `RemovePodSandboxRequest` / `RemovePodSandboxResponse`\n  - Simple request with just the `pod_sandbox_id`\n- `PodSandboxStatus` message contains:\n  - Sandbox ID, state, creation timestamp\n  - Network settings, metadata labels\n  - Linux-specific namespace paths\n\n### Container Messages\n- `CreateContainerRequest` / `CreateContainerResponse`\n- `StartContainerRequest` / `StartContainerResponse`\n- `ContainerStatus` contains state (created, running, exited) and detailed resource info\n\n---\n\n## 3. Generated gRPC Code\n\n### 3.1 gRPC Compilation\nThe proto files are compiled to generate:\n- **File**: `api_grpc.pb.go` - Contains the gRPC service definitions\n- Generated client interface: `RuntimeServiceClient`\n- Generated server interface: `RuntimeServiceServer`\n- Method handlers and registration functions\n\n### 3.2 Server Interface Example\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    Version(context.Context, *VersionRequest) (*VersionResponse, error)\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    StopPodSandbox(context.Context, *StopPodSandboxRequest) (*StopPodSandboxResponse, error)\n    RemovePodSandbox(context.Context, *RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*RemovePodSandboxResponse, error)\n    PodSandboxStatus(context.Context, *PodSandboxStatusRequest) (*PodSandboxStatusResponse, error)\n    // ... other methods\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Registration Function\n```go\nfunc RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s grpc.ServiceRegistrar, srv RuntimeServiceServer) {\n    // Registers all RPC handlers with the gRPC server\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### 4.1 Entry Point: CRI Plugin Registration\n\n**File**: `plugins/cri/cri.go` (containerd repository)\n\nThe containerd CRI plugin is initialized as a gRPC plugin:\n\n```go\nfunc init() {\n    defaultConfig := criconfig.DefaultServerConfig()\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,      // Runtime service\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,      // Sandbox controller\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin,\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,          // Node Resource Interface\n            plugins.EventPlugin,\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,\n        },\n        InitFn: initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 gRPC Server Implementation\n\n**Type**: `criGRPCServer` struct\n\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Embedded interface implementation\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer    // Embedded interface implementation\n    io.Closer\n    initializer                   // IsInitialized() method\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\nThis structure:\n- **Embeds** the gRPC server interfaces from the CRI API\n- **Wraps** them with instrumentation for logging, metrics, and tracing\n- **Registers** both services with the gRPC server\n\n### 4.3 Service Implementation Layer\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe actual implementation is in the `criService` struct:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    RuntimeService    // Embedded dependency\n    ImageService      // Embedded dependency\n\n    // State management\n    config             criconfig.Config\n    sandboxStore       *sandboxstore.Store    // Stores pod sandbox metadata\n    containerStore     *containerstore.Store  // Stores container metadata\n    sandboxNameIndex   *registrar.Registrar   // Ensures unique names\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n\n    // Network and streaming\n    netPlugin          map[string]cni.CNI    // CNI plugin for networking\n    streamServer       streaming.Server      // For exec/attach streams\n\n    // Monitoring and integration\n    eventMonitor       *events.EventMonitor  // Container event tracking\n    nri                *nri.API              // Node Resource Interface\n    sandboxService     sandboxService        // Sandbox controller\n    runtimeHandlers    map[string]*runtime.RuntimeHandler\n    statsCollector     *StatsCollector\n}\n```\n\n### 4.4 Method Implementation Example: RunPodSandbox\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n\n    // 1. Generate unique ID and reserve name to prevent concurrent creation\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    metadata := config.GetMetadata()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n\n    if err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name: %w\", err)\n    }\n    defer func() {\n        if retErr != nil {\n            c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(name)\n        }\n    }()\n\n    // 2. Create lease for resource tracking\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    ls, err := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create lease: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Select OCI runtime based on config and runtime handler\n    ociRuntime, err := c.config.GetSandboxRuntime(config, r.GetRuntimeHandler())\n    if err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to get OCI runtime: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 4. Create sandbox store entry\n    sandbox := sandboxstore.NewSandbox(\n        sandboxstore.Metadata{\n            ID:             id,\n            Name:           name,\n            Config:         config,\n            RuntimeHandler: r.GetRuntimeHandler(),\n        },\n        sandboxstore.Status{\n            State: sandboxstore.StateUnknown,\n        },\n    )\n\n    // 5. Set up networking (CNI)\n    // 6. Start the sandbox via sandbox controller\n    // 7. Trigger NRI hooks for Node Resource Interface\n\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{\n        PodSandboxId: id,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Patterns:\n- **Resource isolation**: Each sandbox gets a lease for resource cleanup\n- **Name reservation**: Prevents concurrent creation of same sandbox\n- **Store management**: Maintains metadata in `sandboxStore` for lifecycle tracking\n- **Error recovery**: Deferred cleanup functions ensure partial failures are rolled back\n- **Instrumentation**: Wrapped with tracing spans and logging\n\n### 4.5 StopPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Look up sandbox in store (idempotent - returns success if not found)\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            // Idempotent: already stopped/removed, return success\n            return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error finding sandbox: %w\", err)\n    }\n\n    // 2. Stop all containers in the sandbox (forced termination)\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.stopContainerRetryOnConnectionClosed(ctx, container, 0); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Stop the sandbox container itself if running or unknown\n    state := sandbox.Status.Get().State\n    if state == sandboxstore.StateReady || state == sandboxstore.StateUnknown {\n        if err := c.sandboxService.StopSandbox(ctx, sandbox.Sandboxer, sandbox.ID); err != nil {\n            if !errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to stop sandbox: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 4. Trigger NRI hooks\n    // 5. Update sandbox state to \"NotReady\"\n\n    return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n#### Key Design Points:\n- **Idempotent semantics**: Returns success even if sandbox already stopped\n- **Cascading shutdown**: Stops all containers first, then the sandbox\n- **State tracking**: Uses internal state to avoid redundant operations\n- **Error handling**: Distinguishes between \"not found\" (ok) and real errors\n\n### 4.6 RemovePodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // 1. Find the sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(r.GetPodSandboxId())\n    if err != nil {\n        if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n            return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n        }\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // 2. Force-remove all containers in the sandbox\n    containers := c.containerStore.List()\n    for _, container := range containers {\n        if container.SandboxID == sandbox.ID {\n            if err := c.removeContainer(ctx, container.ID); err != nil {\n                return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to remove container: %w\", err)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Trigger NRI removal hooks\n    // 4. Release the sandbox name from the index\n    // 5. Delete lease\n    // 6. Remove from sandbox store\n\n    return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Instrumentation Layer\n\n### 5.1 Middleware Pattern\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go`\n\nContainerd wraps the criService with an instrumented service that adds:\n\n```go\ntype instrumentedService struct {\n    c runtime.RuntimeServiceServer  // Wrapped service\n}\n\nfunc (in *instrumentedService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Check if service is initialized\n    if err := in.checkInitialized(); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // Log the request\n    log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox for %+v\", r.GetConfig().GetMetadata())\n\n    // Call the actual implementation\n    res, err := in.c.RunPodSandbox(ctx, r)\n\n    // Log the response or error\n    if err != nil {\n        log.G(ctx).WithError(err).Errorf(\"RunPodSandbox failed\")\n    } else {\n        log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox returns sandbox id %q\", res.GetPodSandboxId())\n    }\n\n    return res, err\n}\n```\n\nThis pattern provides:\n- **Logging**: Detailed request/response logging\n- **Metrics**: Request timing and counts\n- **Tracing**: Distributed tracing spans\n- **Validation**: Server initialization checks\n\n---\n\n## 6. Kubernetes Vendoring of Containerd APIs\n\n### 6.1 Vendor Structure\n\n**Location**: `vendor/github.com/containerd/` (in kubernetes repo)\n\nKubernetes vendors only the **API types** from containerd, not the full implementation:\n\n```\nvendor/github.com/containerd/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 containerd/\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 api/\n\u2502       \u251c\u2500\u2500 services/      # gRPC service definitions\n\u2502       \u2514\u2500\u2500 types/         # Common data types\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 errdefs/              # Error definitions\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 log/                  # Logging interface\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 ttrpc/               # ttrpc protocol implementation\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 typeurl/             # Type URL registry for protobuf\n```\n\n### 6.2 Key Vendored Components\n\n**containerd/api/types**: Core container and sandbox types that represent the container runtime state\n\n**containerd/errdefs**: Error codes that containerd uses:\n- `IsNotFound(err)` - checks if resource doesn't exist\n- `IsAlreadyExists(err)` - resource creation collision\n- `IsInvalidArgument(err)` - malformed request\n- `IsFailedPrecondition(err)` - resource in wrong state\n\nThis error package is critical for the idempotent semantics of CRI operations.\n\n### 6.3 Kubernetes CRI Client\n\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go`\n\nKubernetes implements a client that communicates with containerd via the CRI interface:\n\n```go\ntype remoteRuntimeService struct {\n    runtimeClient runtimeapi.RuntimeServiceClient  // gRPC client\n    timeout       time.Duration\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n        config *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig, runtimeHandler string) (string, error) {\n\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    resp, err := r.runtimeClient.RunPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.RunPodSandboxRequest{\n        Config:         config,\n        RuntimeHandler: runtimeHandler,\n    })\n\n    if err != nil {\n        return \"\", err\n    }\n\n    return resp.PodSandboxId, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *remoteRuntimeService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, podSandBoxID string) error {\n    ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, r.timeout)\n    defer cancel()\n\n    _, err := r.runtimeClient.StopPodSandbox(ctx, &runtimeapi.StopPodSandboxRequest{\n        PodSandboxId: podSandBoxID,\n    })\n\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Interface Contract and Semantics\n\n### 7.1 Idempotent Operations\n\nBoth `StopPodSandbox` and `RemovePodSandbox` are **idempotent**:\n- Multiple calls with same ID should succeed\n- Calling on non-existent resource should return success\n- Kubelet relies on this for reliable cleanup\n\n**Implementation guarantee**: In both containerd and Kubernetes client:\n```\nif err != nil && !isNotFound(err) {\n    return err\n}\n// Return success regardless\n```\n\n### 7.2 Cascading Lifecycle\n\nThe CRI defines a specific lifecycle:\n1. **RunPodSandbox** - Creates and starts sandbox (must be Ready)\n2. **CreateContainer** - Creates containers in the sandbox\n3. **StartContainer** - Starts the containers\n4. **StopContainer** - Stops containers gracefully\n5. **StopPodSandbox** - Stops sandbox (must terminate all containers)\n6. **RemoveContainer** - Removes container metadata\n7. **RemovePodSandbox** - Removes sandbox metadata\n\nContainerd enforces this through state tracking and cascading cleanup.\n\n### 7.3 Graceful vs Forced Termination\n\n- **StopContainer(grace_period)**: Sends SIGTERM, waits for grace period, then SIGKILL\n- **StopPodSandbox**: Forcibly terminates all containers (grace period = 0)\n- **RemovePodSandbox**: Forcibly removes all containers\n\n### 7.4 Resource Cleanup\n\nThree levels of resource management:\n1. **Leases** (containerd): Automatic cleanup of orphaned resources\n2. **Stores** (criService): In-memory tracking of sandbox/container metadata\n3. **CNI plugins**: Network namespace cleanup on sandbox removal\n\n---\n\n## 8. Message Flow Example: Create and Run Pod\n\n### Complete Request-Response Chain\n\n```\nKubelet Requests:\n1. RunPodSandbox(config)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.RunPodSandbox()\n   \u2192 Creates lease, reserves name, creates sandbox store entry\n   \u2192 Calls sandboxService.StartSandbox() with OCI runtime\n   \u2192 Returns sandbox_id\n   Response: RunPodSandboxResponse { pod_sandbox_id = \"abc123\" }\n\n2. CreateContainer(sandbox_id, config)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.CreateContainer()\n   \u2192 Creates container store entry\n   \u2192 Generates OCI spec from config\n   Response: CreateContainerResponse { container_id = \"def456\" }\n\n3. StartContainer(container_id)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.StartContainer()\n   \u2192 Calls sandboxService.StartTask() to run OCI runtime\n   Response: StartContainerResponse {}\n\n4. PodSandboxStatus(sandbox_id)\n   \u2192 gRPC call to containerd CRI service\n   \u2192 criService.PodSandboxStatus()\n   \u2192 Returns sandbox state from store\n   Response: PodSandboxStatusResponse { status = SANDBOX_READY, ... }\n\nLater for cleanup:\n5. StopContainer(container_id, grace_period)\n   \u2192 Sends SIGTERM, waits, then SIGKILL\n   Response: StopContainerResponse {}\n\n6. RemoveContainer(container_id)\n   Response: RemoveContainerResponse {}\n\n7. StopPodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   \u2192 Stops all containers in sandbox\n   \u2192 Stops sandbox container\n   Response: StopPodSandboxResponse {}\n\n8. RemovePodSandbox(sandbox_id)\n   \u2192 Removes all containers\n   \u2192 Releases name reservation\n   \u2192 Deletes lease\n   \u2192 Removes from store\n   Response: RemovePodSandboxResponse {}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Error Handling\n\n### 9.1 Error Types from Kubernetes CRI Spec\n\nAll operations return gRPC errors that map to error codes:\n- `Unimplemented` - Method not supported\n- `Internal` - Unexpected runtime error\n- `InvalidArgument` - Bad request parameters\n- `AlreadyExists` - Resource already created\n- `NotFound` - Resource doesn't exist\n- `FailedPrecondition` - Resource in wrong state\n\n### 9.2 Idempotency Handling\n\nContainerd's idempotent error handling:\n```go\n// In StopPodSandbox\nsandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(id)\nif err != nil {\n    if errdefs.IsNotFound(err) {\n        return &StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil  // Success even if not found\n    }\n    return nil, err  // Real error\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Architecture Summary\n\n### 10.1 Layered Design\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Kubernetes kubelet                              \u2502\n\u2502 (CRI client - runtime.RuntimeServiceClient)     \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                   \u2502 gRPC calls over Unix socket\n                   \u2502\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25bc\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Containerd CRI Plugin (plugins/cri/cri.go)      \u2502\n\u2502 \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510   \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502 criGRPCServer                            \u2502   \u2502\n\u2502 \u2502 - Containerd's implementation demonstrates:\n\n1. **Correct semantics**: Implements idempotent operations as specified\n2. **Robust state management**: Uses stores and leases to prevent resource leaks\n3. **Graceful error handling**: Distinguishes between expected and unexpected errors\n4. **Extensibility**: Supports runtime selection, plugins (NRI), and event streaming\n5. **Observability**: Multi-layer instrumentation for debugging and monitoring\n\nThe interface contract is enforced through gRPC's strongly-typed message definitions, allowing Kubernetes and containerd to evolve independently while maintaining compatibility through the CRI protocol versioning system.\n",

# Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) Trace Analysis

## Overview

This document traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition through containerd's implementation. The analysis spans both the Kubernetes and containerd repositories, mapping the interface contract to concrete implementation.

---

## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition

### 1.1 Definition Location
**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`

The Kubernetes project maintains the Container Runtime Interface as a protocol buffer specification with gRPC service definitions. This is the source of truth for all container runtime implementations.

### 1.2 Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService

The CRI RuntimeService gRPC interface defines the following key RPC methods:

#### Sandbox Lifecycle Operations
```protobuf
service RuntimeService {
    // Version returns the runtime name, runtime version, and runtime API version.
    rpc Version(VersionRequest) returns (VersionResponse) {}

    // RunPodSandbox creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes must ensure
    // the sandbox is in the ready state on success.
    rpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}

    // StopPodSandbox stops any running process that is part of the sandbox and
    // reclaims network resources (e.g., IP addresses) allocated to the sandbox.
    // If there are any running containers in the sandbox, they must be forcibly
    // terminated. This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if all
    // relevant resources have already been reclaimed.
    rpc StopPodSandbox(StopPodSandboxRequest) returns (StopPodSandboxResponse) {}

    // RemovePodSandbox removes the sandbox. If there are any running containers
    // in the s
... (truncated)
